posted:Posted March 24, 2024
msg:If you don't go to the crowded Dinosaur Park, Zhongwu Hotel is the spring garden. The end of the luxury brand, the state guesthouse, the super large garden, the well-built roads make me miss my folding bicycle, the flowers in the rain, the garden after the rain, the pavilions in the sunny day, the bridge under the sunset, it's really fun to visit.

Service
Very good, I was quite worried after reading the reviews before, but I actually felt the warm, professional, and very good service. I arrived at the hotel at 11 o'clock in the morning, and the beautiful Miss Luo Qian at the front desk checked in. The room was ready in advance. Someone helped with the luggage and there were small toys for the children. The welcome fruit in the room is the best among the many five-star hotels recently. It's not that it's so high-end, but each one is fresh and delicious, not just for show and posing for traffic lights.

Facilities
The great swimming pool is my favorite. It is really luxurious to get up in the morning and enjoy the 50-meter large swimming pool alone. The hot spring pool comparable to the main swimming pool of other hotels is a paradise for walking children

Breakfast has local red plum yogurt, the noodles are very good, the noodles are made of lard and soy sauce, and the red soup noodles are made of vegetables. It is the opposite of the vegetarian scallion oil noodles and meat red soup Aozao noodles that Shanghai likes. I chatted with the auntie who cooked the noodles. The noodles were cooked quite standardly, with a little bit of raw core, not too much or too little, just a little bit. Too much is too hard, too little is too soft. The noodles in the north rely on the noodles, and they are chewy no matter how they are cooked. The noodles here rely on the fire. The gestures of the auntie who cooks the noodles are like the back of a crucian carp.

Children's playground
It is quite big and clean. Because of this, it is not all guests. Just play around

The lounge is the lounge with the least people I have visited recently. The service is very good. At first, I thought the dishes were very small, but later I found out that there were only three of us, and we couldn't finish this amount. There are all kinds of freshly fried foods, pasta, Chinese and Western cold dishes. Just a bite and a chat are enough.
